    function make_tooltip(selector){
        /*  Fonction pour gÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â©nÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â©rer un tooltip ÃƒÆ’   partir d'un sÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â©lecteur
            Chaque ÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â©ement renvoyÃƒÆ’Ã‚Â© par le selecteur doit avoir un attribut data-tt qui contient
            - soit le html du tooltip (auquel la fonction ajoute la croix pour la version mobile)
            - soit un argument ÃƒÆ’  passer ÃƒÆ’  une fonction (func) de formattage
            L'argument func est optionnel.
            Il renvoie ÃƒÆ’  une fonction ÃƒÆ’  utiliser pour formatter.
        */
        const isInApp = window.location.href.match(/apps.([a-z]+\-)?lemonde.fr/);
        let tooltip_elmts = getA(selector);
        forEach(tooltip_elmts, function(elmt){
            elmt.addEventListener('mouseover', function(){
                let tooltip = document.createElement('div');
                tooltip.classList.add("tooltipdecodeurs")
                if(isInApp){
                    tooltip.classList.add("aec")
                }
`;
                document.body.appendChild(tooltip)
                tooltip.style.top = this.getBoundingClientRect().top - tooltip.offsetHeight - 20 + 'px'
                tooltip.style.left = this.getBoundingClientRect().left + this.getBoundingClientRect().width/2 - tooltip.getBoundingClientRect().width/2 + 'px'
 this.remove());
            })
            elmt.addEventListener('mouseout', function(){
                let tooltip = document.querySelector('.tooltipdecodeurs');
                if(tooltip != null)
                    tooltip.remove()
            })
        })
    }

    function writeStraightArrow(svg_selector, className, x1, y1, x2, y2, texts){
      const svg_selection = d3.select(svg_selector);
      // Create fleche right
      const trois_points = [
              {x: x1, y: y1},
              {x: x2, y: y2}];
 d.x).y(d => d.y);
      const triangle = "M 0 0 8 4 0 8 0 4";
      d3.select("svg").append("svg:defs").append("svg:marker")
          .attr("class", "d_arrow")
          .attr("id", "triangleFleche-"+className)
          .attr("refX", 1)
          .attr("refY", 4)
          .attr("markerWidth", 8)
          .attr("markerHeight", 8)
          .attr("markerUnits", "userSpaceOnUse")
          .attr("orient", "auto")
          .append("path")
          .attr("d", triangle);
      const group_arrow = svg_selection.append("g").attr("class", className);
      group_arrow.append("path").attr("class", "d_arrow")
          .data([trois_points])
          .attr("d", line_gen)
          .attr("stroke-linecap", "round")
          .attr("marker-end", `url(#triangleFleche-${className})`)
          .attr("fill", "none");

      let i = 0;
      const decalage = 15;
      const n = texts.length;
      for (let text of texts){
            group_arrow.append("text").attr("class", "d_arrow " + className)
                          .text(text)
                          .attr("x", (x1 + x2) / 2)
                          .attr("y", (y1 + y2) / 2 - (n - i) * decalage - (((className === "lula")&&(isMobile))? 40:0))
                          .attr("text-anchor", (className !== "bolsonaro")?(className === "lula")?"start":"middle":"end")
                          .attr("alignment-baseline", "middle");
            i ++;
      }

  }

  writeStraightArrow("svg g.bars", "lula", xScale(2005), yScale(30000), xScale(2010) + xScale.bandwidth() / 2, yScale(10000),
      ["Pendant la prÃ©sidence de Lula,", "la dÃ©forestation annuelle avait diminuÃ©", "de presque 70 %"])

  writeStraightArrow("svg g.bars", "bolsonaro", xScale(2019), yScale(12000), xScale(2021) + xScale.bandwidth() / 2, yScale(14000),
      ["Durant celle", "de Bolsonaro,", "elle a augmentÃ©", "de plus de 70 %"])

          group.append("text").attr("class", "d_arrow")
